                       <div data-reactid="1222">
                        <div data-reactid="1223">
                         Private and modern studio located in a residential neighborhood in Mar Vista. Within close proximity to Abbott Kinney street, Venice beach and canals and Santa Monica. Private entrance, bathroom and ample street parking. A lovely retreat.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1224">
                         Bright and airy modern guesthouse, situated behind a private home in a residential neighborhood in Mar Vista--centrally located in west Los Angeles. It has a private entrance and bathroom with a shower. There is a mini kitchenette which includes a sink, small fridge and a electric tea kettle. PLEASE NOTE that there is not a stove or any appliances to prepare meals. We also provide a very high quality alkaline water from our filter inside our house. The unit has a cathedral ceiling, skylights and a beautiful blond bamboo floor. Please note that although there ARE privacy curtains around the studio, there are no black out curtains, so it does get pretty light filled in the morning due to the skylights and other high windows. Entrance is through a pedestrian gate on the side of the main house. The unit is surrounded by a beautifully landscaped yard that includes mature trees, a waterfall and pond--certain times of year you will see lotus blossoms in the pond! Just outside the unit is a gas fire pit that makes for lovely romantic evenings under the stars-perhaps a glass of wine? We have 2 young children that play in the backyard and jump on the trampoline nearby the unit. We will do our best to honor our guests privacy and quietude--we have a playground for them in the front yard too but it is important to note that this is a home with kids :) There is ample street parking and we will provide all guests with a parking permit. For those without a car we are a minute walk to Venice Blvd and various bus lines. We are about a mile away from famous Abbott Kinney Street and 2 miles from Venice beach and the canals so its a quick drive otherwise we have 2 bikes that make for a nice way to explore the oceanfront without dealing with parking. We are within easy access to the 10 and 405 freeways for those wanting to explore the greater LA area. Mar Vista is bordered by Venice, Santa Monica and Culver City so it really is a great central location. We are walking distance from Mitsuwa Japanese market, coffee shops, Chase bank and CVS as well as the Sunday Farmers market. There are two Thai restaurants, an Indian and an all organic cafe/coffee shop within one mile from us. Vons is a 5 minute drive or a 15 minute walk and Whole foods is a less than 10 minute drive away. For guests staying for longer periods of time we can provide access to our washer and dryer. We hope to make your stay as pleasant as possible and will help you in any way we can. We are located in a quiet residential neighborhood and would like to keep it that way so please no inquiries from people interested in a place to party.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1225">
                         The unit is located in a quiet residential neighborhood with easy access to food, shopping and public transportation.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="1462">
                         This is a cozy 1950's built, 2 bedroom 1 bathroom house, with a pleasant, peaceful and private outdoor patio space in the front, and a deck in the back. This home has been renovated with vaulted ceilings, hardwood floors, and french doors.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1463">
                         Walk through the tall redwood gates of this home and follow the tile path to the front door. To the left before entering the home you see a half circle shaped deck protruding out from the house, and on it a picnic table for meal gatherings in the outdoor. When entering the home you will find yourself in a large open room, much in the style of a studio, where the kitchen, dining room, and living room all share the same space, creating a spacious flow of light, air, and energy. To the left of the entry door, on the same wall you'll find french doors that open out to the front deck, allowing for greater light and air circulation. Down the only hallway to the right is the bathroom, where one can enjoy a relaxing epson salt bath after a long day. On the other side of the hallway you will find the laundry room, which then leads into the master bedroom. Both bedrooms have french doors that open to the back deck. The back deck doesn't feel as private as the front deck, since it boarders my neighbors but is still optimal for lounging. *Bookings run on a first come first serve basis, and no holds are placed until a reservation is paid for.
                        </div>

                         The neighborhood is safe and residential.

                        <div data-reactid="1595">
                         QUIET, CREATIVE SPACE, GARDEN GUEST HOUSE - CLOSE TO EVERYTHING (Seriously -close to just about everything you want to see in Los Angeles!) Why stay in a hotel or even a room in someone else’s home, when for the same price (or less) you can have complete privacy in an incredible space. Location: Private guest house which is centrally located in the Culver City/mid-Wilshire adjacent area of Los Angeles. 10 minutes from the charm of Larchmont Village and Paramount Studios, 15 minutes from downtown LA and 7 minutes to Beverly Hills or Culver City. Walking distance to Venice Boulevard which is serviced by major bus lines going east and west., and La Cienega for North/South bus. I've lived her since 1993 and find it to be safe &amp; a typical urban middle class family residential area. Description: The guest house is a newly remodeled 1 room with bathroom and wetbar with its own entry and patio. It is completely detached from the main house ensuring total privacy and is located in a fully gated/fenced backyard. My guests are ensured of their privacy and comfort. I was a professional Travel Host in my my former life and was considered one of the top travel hosts with over 1,000 positive reviews from guests on trips I hosted for that company. I want my guests to feel at home. I love hosting people of all ages and from all parts of the globe. I grew up in Yokohama, Japan and come from an Irish-American heritage, and appreciate all cultures; life would be so dull if we were all the same! Features include: • Lovely and comfortable FULL sized bed with fresh linens on arrival. • Large desk area. • Newly designed all tile bathroom with a double head shower (no tub). Soft and fluffy towels and a hair dryer and iron (upon request) and a professional clothes steamer. • It is bright and cheerful. • The wet bar has a small refrigerator, microwave, electric tea kettle, toaster, blender, French Press, dishes, glasses, cups, cutlery etc. • Free broadband wireless. • Heat (space), no air conditioning (generally not needed considering location to beach &amp; coastal breeze) but has two ceiling fans (if we have a heat wave then it does get hot, but it's rare for this area not to get cold at night... but then again I can't control weather). • Steam cleaned between guests to reduce allergens for those who suffer from seasonal allergies. *Laundry Room on property with coin operated MayTag washer &amp; dryer. Special Conditions: • PLEASE NOTE THE FOLLOWING BEFORE YOU BOOK I require a $200 refundable damage/security deposit and a departure cleaning fee (priced as listed with Airbnb) – both amounts are handled through Airbnb. Cleaning fee does not include taking out your trash or doing dishes. If bags of trash or dirty dishes are left or place is excessively dirty additional cleaning fees will be deducted from security deposit. I will provide you with my housekeepers phone number should you want to hire her services during your stay, but also some cleaning supplies are in the unit so you can do your own cleaning if you're here for an extended stay. Extended stay guest here for 30 days or more will be required to pay for mid-stay cleaning every 14 days and will be charged $55 per cleaning through Airbnb 'Special Amenities' when available but this feature seems to appear and disappear. NO SMOKING inside the house- but you may smoke outside just don't leave butts around. No pets please - I'm doing my best to keep allergy free units. To keep your Airbnb fees down the 14% LA CITY HOTEL TAX on stays 29 days or less must be paid in cash upon arrival. Stays of 30 or more days are considered a rental by the city so are not subject to the tax. I require photos and profiles from all guests - I will not process a booking without this. Check out 10am check in 2pm but flexible to individual needs if doable.
